; --- INDEX ---
;
; lines starting with ; as first non-whitespace are comments
;
; File format is single lines formatted as Key:Value
;
; KEYS
; page:comic page ID and link: heads a comic page entry.
; 	auth: Author / artist page comment or note
; 	date: date of the page, preferably YYYY-MM-DD
; 	desc: text relevant to the page (title / description / line of dialogue, etc)
; 	note: footnotes, links, etc
; 	tag: tags for the page's story items of note: character, item, location, etc.
; baseurl: default url applies to any following page:without a url: key
; (to insert pageID replace in baseurl/url with {0} )
;
; Can use multiple tag: per page, but only one of each of the other keys
;
; desc:, note: and auth: text's internal formatting is a mix of [Markdown](http://daringfireball.net/projects/markdown) plus html (for <br> etc)
; **bold**
; _italic_
; [internal link text](#sometag) - tag links are lower case
; [external link text](http://www.gunnerkrigg.com)
; tags starting ch-* are treated separately as chapter identifiers
;
baseurl: http://wapsisquare.com/comic/{0}/
; Amanda
